5:22:585 hours, 22 minutes, 58 secondscrack open and in the opening they found the books of the master which contained three mystic axioms. Nature pleases
5:23:055 hours, 23 minutes, 5 secondsherself in nature. Nature triumphs over nature. Nature governs nature.

5:23:205 hours, 23 minutes, 20 secondsaffinity lying behind the symbolism which moreover our examination of the hermetic art has already foreshadowed will be treated later. We could also
5:23:295 hours, 23 minutes, 29 secondsposit a psychological interreation in the form of an eeteological assumption according to the terminology of psychoanalysis.

6:05:416 hours, 5 minutes, 41 secondsthis symbolism as we observe most clearly in hypnogogic or half-dreaming hallucinations and in dreams three different groups of objects are represented.
6:05:516 hours, 5 minutes, 51 secondsOne, thought contents. Imagination contents. In brief, the contents or objects of thinking and imagining the
6:05:596 hours, 5 minutes, 59 secondsmaterial of thought, whether it be conscious or unconscious.

6:06:116 hours, 6 minutes, 11 secondsfunctioning of the psyche, whether it be conscious or unconscious.
6:06:166 hours, 6 minutes, 16 secondsThree somatic processes or bodily stimulations.
6:06:216 hours, 6 minutes, 21 secondsThis third sort of objects is closely coordinated with the other two. It is not capable of interesting us in the present connection. So we pass it by.
6:06:306 hours, 6 minutes, 30 secondsTherefore we arrive at two categories in which we can enroll all symbolizing works of the imagination. The material and the functional.
6:06:396 hours, 6 minutes, 39 secondsOne. The material category is characterized by its representation of thought contents, for example, of contents that are worked out in a train of thoughts, arranged thought imagined,
6:06:516 hours, 6 minutes, 51 secondswhether they are mere images or groups of images, concepts that are somewhat drawn out into comparisons and definition processes, or indeed
6:07:006 hours, 7 minutesjudgments, trains of reasoning, which serve as analytic or synthetic operations, etc. Since as we know the fantasies, dreams,
6:07:096 hours, 7 minutes, 9 secondsreveries, even poems are mostly inspired by wishes, it will prove frequently the case that the contents symbolically
6:07:166 hours, 7 minutes, 16 secondscontained in them are wish images. In other words, the imagined experiencing of gratification.
6:07:226 hours, 7 minutes, 22 secondsTwo, the functional category is characterized by the fact that the condition, structure, or capacity for work of the individual consciousness or
6:07:326 hours, 7 minutes, 32 secondsthe psychic apparatus is itself portrayed. It is termed functional because it has nothing to do with the material or the contents of the act of
6:07:406 hours, 7 minutes, 40 secondsthinking but applies merely to manner and method in which consciousness functions. Rapid, slow, easy, hard,
6:07:486 hours, 7 minutes, 48 secondsobstructed, careless, joyful, forced,
6:07:516 hours, 7 minutes, 51 secondsfruitless, successful, disunited, split into complexes, united, interchangeable,
6:07:586 hours, 7 minutes, 58 secondstroubled, etc. It is immaterial whether these are conscious or unconscious.
6:08:046 hours, 8 minutes, 4 secondsThinking must be taken here in the widest possible sense. That means here all psychic processes that can have
6:08:106 hours, 8 minutes, 10 secondsanything as an object. Two typical examples will enable us at once clearly to understand the two categories and
6:08:176 hours, 8 minutes, 17 secondskeep them separate. A material symbolism conditions in a drowsy state I reflect upon the
6:08:266 hours, 8 minutes, 26 secondsnature of the judgments that are transubjectively or for all men valid.

6:08:516 hours, 8 minutes, 51 secondsInterpretation in this symbol everything that I was thinking of is expressed. The validity of the trans sububjective concerns all
6:08:596 hours, 8 minutes, 59 secondsmen without exception. The circle goes through all the heads. This validity must have its cause and something common
6:09:066 hours, 9 minutes, 6 secondsto all. The heads all belong to the same apparently homogeneous sphere. Not all judgments are transubs.
6:09:156 hours, 9 minutes, 15 secondsMen are outside of and under the sphere and stand on the earth as separate individuals.

6:11:046 hours, 11 minutes, 4 secondsaccessible, but we can generally find cases where long contexts of images are susceptible of material as well as

6:12:346 hours, 12 minutes, 34 secondsan above and a below. And for this reason, Mephostophles can say to Fa on his departure, "Plunge, then I could as well say," sore.

6:13:436 hours, 13 minutes, 43 secondsof symbolism. I refer to my studies on symbolism and on dreams in the bibliography.

6:14:126 hours, 14 minutes, 12 secondsBoth lines of interpretation are supplied by the same fabric of images indeed often by the same elements of this image fabric. This context
6:14:216 hours, 14 minutes, 21 secondstherefore must have been sought out artfully enough by the creative unconscious to answer the double requirement.
6:14:286 hours, 14 minutes, 28 secondsThe coexistence of the material meaning with the functional is not entirely puzzling to the student of psychoanalysis.
6:14:356 hours, 14 minutes, 35 secondsTwo facts must be kept in mind throughout. In the first place we are acquainted with the principle of multiple determination or condensation.
6:14:446 hours, 14 minutes, 44 secondsThe multiplicity of the dimly moving latent dream thoughts condenses into a few clear dream forms or symbols so that
6:14:516 hours, 14 minutes, 51 secondsone symbol continually as it were appears as the representative of several ideas and is therefore interpretable in
6:14:596 hours, 14 minutes, 59 secondsseveral ways. that it should be susceptible of more than one interpretation can cause no surprise because the fundamental significance,
6:15:086 hours, 15 minutes, 8 secondsthe latent thoughts were the very ones that by association caused the selection of the symbols from an infinite series
6:15:156 hours, 15 minutes, 15 secondsof possibilities in the shaping of the dream and therefore in the unconscious dream work only such pictorial elements
6:15:226 hours, 15 minutes, 22 secondscould penetrate into consciousness as satisfied the requirements of the multiple determination.
6:15:296 hours, 15 minutes, 29 secondsThe principle of multiple determination is valid not only within the material and the functional categories, but makes the fusion of both in the symbol in question to some extent intelligible.
6:15:416 hours, 15 minutes, 41 secondsElements of both categories take an active part in the choice of the symbol.
6:15:456 hours, 15 minutes, 45 secondsOn the one hand, a number of affects press on towards the symbolic representation of objects to which they direct themselves, objects of love,
6:15:546 hours, 15 minutes, 54 secondshate, etc. On the other hand, the psyche takes cognizance of its own impulses,
6:15:596 hours, 15 minutes, 59 secondsplay of a effects, etc. And this perception will gain representation.

8:39:408 hours, 39 minutes, 40 secondsable to place itself in higher developed tales in correspondingly closer connection with mythical material.

8:40:028 hours, 40 minutes, 2 secondseast. The night path of the sun apparently under the sea. He lights a fire in the belly of the animal and cuts off a piece of the pendant heart when he
8:40:118 hours, 40 minutes, 11 secondsfeels hungry. Soon after, he notices that the fish is running a ground. The real sun comes up to the horizon from
8:40:188 hours, 40 minutes, 18 secondsbelow. He begins immediately to cut his way out of the animal and then slips out, which is sunrise. In the belly of
8:40:268 hours, 40 minutes, 26 secondsthe fish, it has become so hot that all his hair has fallen out. Hair probably signifies rays. Quite as clear as the
8:40:348 hours, 40 minutes, 34 secondsnature myth perport is the fact that we have a representation of regeneration which is quite as conceivable in psychoanalytic as an anagogic explanation.

8:48:268 hours, 48 minutes, 26 secondsSection two, the goal of the work.

8:50:338 hours, 50 minutes, 33 secondsThe alchemistic process is as the hermetics themselves say a cyclical work and the resides to a certain degree in

8:51:388 hours, 51 minutes, 38 secondsBut this agreement is restricted to some principles of vital significance in their doctrine which have reference almost exclusively to a definite
8:51:468 hours, 51 minutes, 46 secondspractice probably to a complete setting to work of the consciousness of duty which is what Kant claims to do with
8:51:538 hours, 51 minutes, 53 secondsthis categorical imperative. an unreasoning, though not unreasonable,
8:51:588 hours, 51 minutes, 58 secondsobedience to an experienced imperious sense of duty, leaving the result to God. And this I am disposed to call the way.
8:52:088 hours, 52 minutes, 8 secondsDo thy duty, ask not after the result of thy doing, without dependence thereon, carry out that which is thy duty.
8:52:168 hours, 52 minutes, 16 secondsWhoever acts without attachment to the world, that man attains the loftiest goal. and the like in many places in the
8:52:248 hours, 52 minutes, 24 secondsBhagavad Gita. Now the end is perhaps the fruit of this obedience. It may be that the steady preservation of the
8:52:318 hours, 52 minutes, 31 secondsinward unity which regards with composure all external vicissitudes leads man finally to some special experience by which a seal of
8:52:408 hours, 52 minutes, 40 secondsconfirmation is set upon what was first a mere trust in the ultimate blessing of rectitude. The hermetic philosophers
8:52:478 hours, 52 minutes, 47 secondswould have the conscious known as the way or as the base of the work. But with regard to the peculiar wonderwork of alchemy or transmutation, they place the
8:52:578 hours, 52 minutes, 57 secondschief value on love. It affects the transformation of the subject into the object loved. Arabi. It is a fundamental
8:53:068 hours, 53 minutes, 6 secondsprinciple of love that thou becomest the real essence of the beloved God in that thou givest up thy individuality and
8:53:148 hours, 53 minutes, 14 secondsdisappearest in him. Blessedness is the abiding place of the divine and holy joy.

8:54:428 hours, 54 minutes, 42 secondspassage, he says, "Play denotes the various states of the mystic to which he is advanced when he passes from one divine name to another. It is the
8:54:528 hours, 54 minutes, 52 secondsethical idea of the mystic more and more to put off the limited ego and to take on in its place the qualities of God in
8:54:598 hours, 54 minutes, 59 secondsorder to become God. When with Arabi the theme of an ode is through aseticism fervent yearning after God and patience
8:55:078 hours, 55 minutes, 7 secondsand suffering man becomes God or acquires divine nature. Then this goal is identical with that of the alchemistic transmutation. The base metal acquires after purification,
8:55:198 hours, 55 minutes, 19 secondsrefining etc. by virtue of the tincturing with the philosopher's stone the nature of gold. In other
8:55:258 hours, 55 minutes, 25 secondswords, the divine nature. But patient effort is requisite. Precipitancy is as great an evil as inactivity. It is, to
8:55:348 hours, 55 minutes, 34 secondsuse the language of the alchemists, just as bad to scorch the tender blossoms by a forced and hasty fire, that in spite
8:55:418 hours, 55 minutes, 41 secondsof its intensity, may be merely a straw fire, as to let go out the fire which should be continuously kept alike, and to let grow cold the materia.
8:55:528 hours, 55 minutes, 52 secondsThe process of distillation is to be accomplished slowly, so that the spirits may not escape. That which rises as steam through the heating in the
8:56:018 hours, 56 minutes, 1 secondreceptacle. In other words, in man is the soul rising into the higher regions.
8:56:078 hours, 56 minutes, 7 secondsDistilling like raindrops, distiller equaling drop down. It brings each time to the thirsting materia a divine gain.
8:56:168 hours, 56 minutes, 16 secondsBut this process is not to be overdone.
8:56:188 hours, 56 minutes, 18 secondsFor the thirsting earth must be gently instilled with the heavenly moisture of the water of life, the process of imbibition.
8:56:278 hours, 56 minutes, 27 secondsThe metallic subject must be gently dissolved in its own natural water or conscience, not with powerful media, not
8:56:348 hours, 56 minutes, 34 secondswith corroding acids, which the foolish employ in order to reach the goal in a hurry, for by such means he either spoils the materia, or produces a merely

8:57:548 hours, 57 minutes, 54 secondsAnd because the conditions of the mastery appear to the Nephite to contradict nature or each other, the mystical experiences that are derived

9:00:159 hours, 15 secondsunconscious are but one, the unknown decreasing as the known increases, and vice versa.

9:02:019 hours, 2 minutes, 1 secondDesire is, as some ancient philosophers think, the root of all affects which manifest themselves in pairs. Joy
9:02:099 hours, 2 minutes, 9 secondscorresponds to desire fulfilled, sorrow to the obstructed or imperiled fulfillment. Hope is the expectation of
9:02:169 hours, 2 minutes, 16 secondsfulfillment, fear the opposite, etc. All the pairs of opposites are in some degree superficial, something that comes

9:02:319 hours, 2 minutes, 31 secondsan ever enduring connation, as it was formerly called. It is the libido of the psychoanalysis. In its manifestations,
9:02:399 hours, 2 minutes, 39 secondsit is subjected to bipolarity, as steckle has named in the inevitable pairs of opposites.

9:02:549 hours, 2 minutes, 54 secondsambiguous expressions for a hostile disas or couple with whose removal a better condition first commences.

9:03:109 hours, 3 minutes, 10 secondsis full of agony on account of the pairs of opposites which are to be found everywhere. Heat cold, high, low, good,
9:03:199 hours, 3 minutes, 19 secondsevil, joy, sorrow, poor, rich, young,
9:03:249 hours, 3 minutes, 24 secondsold, etc. The basis of the opposites is formed by the primal opposition, Rajasthamus.
9:03:319 hours, 3 minutes, 31 secondsto escape from it and recognizing the true ego as superior to it and not participating in it is the foremost purpose of the effort towards salvation.
9:03:409 hours, 3 minutes, 40 secondsSo whoever has raised himself above the qualities of substances is described as having escaped from opposites.
9:03:489 hours, 3 minutes, 48 secondsContact of atoms is only cold and warm,
9:03:519 hours, 3 minutes, 51 secondsbrings pleasure and pain. They come and go without permanency.
9:03:569 hours, 3 minutes, 56 secondsTolerate them, oh Barata, the wise man whom these do not affect. Oh mighty hero who bears pain and pleasure with
9:04:039 hours, 4 minutes, 3 secondsequinimity. He is ripening for immortality.
9:04:099 hours, 4 minutes, 9 secondsThe spirit, the true ego is raised above the agitation of the qualities of nature.
9:04:159 hours, 4 minutes, 15 secondsSwords cut him not. Fire burns him not.
9:04:199 hours, 4 minutes, 19 secondsWater wets him not, nor does the wind wither him. Not to be cut, not to burn,
9:04:259 hours, 4 minutes, 25 secondsnot to get wet, not to be withered. He is constant above everything, continuous, eternal, immovable.
9:04:349 hours, 4 minutes, 34 secondsThis characterization sounds almost like the description of the mercury of the philosophers, which is indestructible, a water that does not wet, a fire that does not consume,
9:04:459 hours, 4 minutes, 45 secondsHermes on the human soul.

9:05:049 hours, 5 minutes, 4 secondssoul, art of one nature, but they are manifold. Thou art but one with thyself.

10:42:0910 hours, 42 minutes, 9 secondsfrom God. And as long as he is in this condition, he is a debtor to sin and under its dominion, which subjects him

10:43:5510 hours, 43 minutes, 55 secondsback, and kept by the strong rock of omnipotence to struggle towards, which with a fresh attack, I resolutely
10:44:0210 hours, 44 minutes, 2 secondsdetermined, and would be sent away with nothing less than the kingdom and the ruling power of the Holy Ghost.
10:44:1010 hours, 44 minutes, 10 secondsIn a parallel between the old and new royal art, I cannot overlook the French Masonic writer Oswald Worth, who has
10:44:1710 hours, 44 minutes, 17 secondsworked in the same province. I agree with him in general, although much of his method of interpretation seems to me too arbitrary. I have already called
10:44:2610 hours, 44 minutes, 26 secondsattention to several passages from WSH on the preparation of the subject, in other words, the uninitiated. I will

10:44:5810 hours, 44 minutes, 58 secondsair test. After descending to the center of the earth, Vita interior ter etc.
10:45:0510 hours, 45 minutes, 5 secondsSmeardine tablet 68 where the roots of all individuality meet. The spirit rises up again. The smearine tablet 10
10:45:1410 hours, 45 minutes, 14 secondsreleased from the caput mortuam which is blocked on the floor of the hermetic receptacle. The residuum is represented by the castoff raignment of the novice.
10:45:2410 hours, 45 minutes, 24 secondsLaboriously now he toils forward in the darkness. The heights draw him on. Escaping hell, he will attain to heaven.
10:45:3210 hours, 45 minutes, 32 secondsHis ascent up the holy mountain is hindered by a violent storm. He is thrown into the depths by the tempest. A symbol of circulation in the closed
10:45:4110 hours, 45 minutes, 41 secondsvessel of the alchemists, which vessel corresponds to the protected lodge.
10:45:4610 hours, 45 minutes, 46 secondsDuring the circulation of the volatile parts, rise and fall again like rain,
10:45:5110 hours, 45 minutes, 51 secondswhich is symbolized by the tears upon the walls. To be sure, it is not here that the Neopight is subjected to the water test. And if a confusion is
10:46:0010 hours, 46 minutespossible on this point, it comes from the fact that all the operations of the great work go on in one vessel, while the Masonic initiation is completed in a
10:46:0910 hours, 46 minutes, 9 secondssuite of different rooms, so that the symbolic series here suffers disintegration.
10:46:1510 hours, 46 minutes, 15 secondsThe circulating water which soaks into the pores of the earthly parts of the subject purifies it more and more so that it goes from gray through a series of colors, the peacock's tail, to white.
10:46:2710 hours, 46 minutes, 27 secondsIn this stage, the material corresponds to the wise man who knows how to resist all seduction. Yet we are not to be

10:46:5610 hours, 46 minutes, 56 secondsnot attained this moral clearness, the light cannot be vouched to him. In brief, in the first degree, the main thing is the comprehensive purification.
10:47:0610 hours, 47 minutes, 6 secondsThe salt layers must be made crystal clear that surround the inner sulfur like a crust and hinder it from its free
10:47:1310 hours, 47 minutes, 13 secondsradiation. Sulfur is to be regarded as a symbol of the expanse of power as individual initiative as will. Mercury
10:47:2210 hours, 47 minutes, 22 secondsstands opposite to it as woman does to man as that which goes to the subject from without or as absolute receptivity.
10:47:3010 hours, 47 minutes, 30 secondsSalt is midway between both. In it, the equilibrium between sulfur and mercury is found. It is a symbol of what appears
10:47:3810 hours, 47 minutes, 38 secondsas the stable being of man. In the first degree, the purification of the salt is worked out for the release of the
10:47:4510 hours, 47 minutes, 45 secondssulfur. The red column J corresponds to the red sulfur by which symbolically the novice gets their reward. For the rest,
10:47:5410 hours, 47 minutes, 54 secondsthe first degree is satisfied with getting the noviceses to see the universal light, the blazing star.
10:48:0010 hours, 48 minutesThe fire test takes place in the second degree. The fiery sulfur must be worked out or rather sent out and used for
10:48:0710 hours, 48 minutes, 7 secondswork. The field of activity of the member proportions itself as it were according to the expansion or range of its sulfurous radiation. At this time
10:48:1710 hours, 48 minutes, 17 secondsthe member enters into a relation of such intensified activity with the world that the intellectual grasp which corresponds to the mercury equaling
10:48:2510 hours, 48 minutes, 25 secondsprinciple acquires from it a new illumination or blazing star and breaks away for a connection of the will which
10:48:3210 hours, 48 minutes, 32 secondswas at first merely individual with the collectivity.
10:48:3610 hours, 48 minutes, 36 secondsTo me at least that appears to be the sense of the figurative but not quite clear exposition of WSH which I have for
10:48:4410 hours, 48 minutes, 44 secondsthe sake of exactness given in the original context.
10:48:4810 hours, 48 minutes, 48 secondsAs soon as the crude stone is cut and polished, we have no longer to work inward but outward. What we are to accomplish so creatively would be
10:48:5710 hours, 48 minutes, 57 secondsinsignificant if we did not know the secret of borrowing power from a power that apparently lies without us. Where
10:49:0410 hours, 49 minutes, 4 secondsdo these mysterious powers work if not at the pillar Boaz? In the north,
10:49:0910 hours, 49 minutes, 9 secondsdirected on the contrary towards the moon, whose soft feminine light it reflects, it corresponds to Mercury,
10:49:1510 hours, 49 minutes, 15 secondswhich unceasingly flows towards all being in order to support its central fire. The exaltation of the latter leads
10:49:2310 hours, 49 minutes, 23 secondsto the fire test, the idea of which worth seems to take in strictly occult form in the manner of Elephice Levy.
10:49:3010 hours, 49 minutes, 30 secondsFinally, a circulation takes place in that the individual will seeks like a magnet to draw the divine will. Always
10:49:3710 hours, 49 minutes, 37 secondsfalls down again, rises, however, and so on in cycles till both meet in the philosophical fire. It is the cycle of which we read in the smearine tablet.
10:49:4710 hours, 49 minutes, 47 secondsThe incombustible essence that comes forth from the fire test is the phoenix, a figure much used by the alchemists.
10:49:5410 hours, 49 minutes, 54 secondsThe member has the task of changing himself into the phoenix. Not only fire belongs to the work however but also the act must be guided by intelligence.
10:50:0410 hours, 50 minutes, 4 secondsActivity and receptivity must complement each other. Therefore the member has to know both pillars thoroughly and
10:50:1110 hours, 50 minutes, 11 secondstherefore he becomes also the already mentioned androgynous material reebus.
10:50:1610 hours, 50 minutes, 16 secondsThat is only to be attained when the elemental propensities are overcome.
10:50:2010 hours, 50 minutes, 20 secondsTherefore the figure reebus is represented as standing on the dragon.
10:50:2610 hours, 50 minutes, 26 secondsWhat will the master do now? He will identify himself with the master builder of all worlds in order to work in him
10:50:3310 hours, 50 minutes, 33 secondsand through him. When anyone says that that is mysticism, he is not wrong.
10:50:3810 hours, 50 minutes, 38 secondsBeing developed on the three successive ways of purgatio, illuminatio, and yuno,
10:50:4410 hours, 50 minutes, 44 secondsthis mysticism is no less logical than the religious mysticism that with its mortifications, if it were only rightly understood, would accomplish the same
10:50:5310 hours, 50 minutes, 53 secondspurpose. Mortification is, as the word itself says, the endeavor for a certain kind of death. Twice is the mason
10:51:0010 hours, 51 minutesenjoined to die. At the beginning in the preparation room, and at the end, at the final initiation into the inmost
10:51:0710 hours, 51 minutes, 7 secondschamber. The second death corresponds to the perfection of the grand mastery. It signifies the complete sacrifice of his
10:51:1510 hours, 51 minutes, 15 secondspersonality, the renunciation of every personal desire. It is the easement of that radical egotism that caused the
10:51:2210 hours, 51 minutes, 22 secondsfall of Adam in that he dragged down spirituality into capore reality. The narrow pucilanimous ego melts into
10:51:3010 hours, 51 minutes, 30 secondsnothing before the high impersonal self symbolized by Hyram, the mythical sins of the eternal universal human atom are thus expatiated.
10:51:4010 hours, 51 minutes, 40 secondsThe architect of the temples is to the grandmaster builder of all worlds. Just what in Christian symbolism the word become flesh is to the eternal father.
10:51:5010 hours, 51 minutes, 50 secondsIn order to carry on the work of the universal structure with advantage, the master must enter into the closest union of the will with God. No longer a slave
10:51:5910 hours, 51 minutes, 59 secondsin anything, he is the more a master of all. The more his will works in harmony with the one that rules the universe.
10:52:0710 hours, 52 minutes, 7 secondsplaced between the abstract and the concrete, between the creative intelligence and the objective creation.
10:52:1310 hours, 52 minutes, 13 secondsMan thus conceived appears like the mediator par excellence or the veritable demiurge of the gnostics. Yet it is not
10:52:2110 hours, 52 minutes, 21 secondsenough that he gets light from its original source. He must also be bound by endless activity to those whom he is to lead. The necessary bond is sympathy,
10:52:3210 hours, 52 minutes, 32 secondslove. The master must make himself loved and he can only succeed by himself loving with all the warmth of a
10:52:3910 hours, 52 minutes, 39 secondsgenerosity extending even to absolute devotion even to the sacrifice of himself. The pelican we are already
10:52:4610 hours, 52 minutes, 46 secondsacquainted with this hermetic bird is the hieroglyph for this loving sacrifice without which every effort remains vain.
10:52:5410 hours, 52 minutes, 54 secondsThe master's degree this necessarily last degree corresponds to an ideal that has set us as a task. We must strive
10:53:0210 hours, 53 minutes, 2 secondstowards it even if its realization is beyond our powers. Our temple will never be finished and no one expects to see the true eternal hyum arise in himself.
10:53:1210 hours, 53 minutes, 12 secondsWe find also in worth how the work is divided into three main steps which begin with the purifying turn towards the inner soul and end with the death
10:53:2210 hours, 53 minutes, 22 secondsresembling yuno mystica. Here we find too in the last degree the unattainable ideal which like a star in heaven shall
10:53:3010 hours, 53 minutes, 30 secondsgive a sure course to the voyage of our life. The viewing of the exalted anagogic conception as a perspective vanishing point makes allowance for the
10:53:3910 hours, 53 minutes, 39 secondspossible errors of superposition in the anagogic aspect of the elementary types.
10:53:4410 hours, 53 minutes, 44 secondsThe tripartite division which we meet in the great work shows the frequently doubted inner qualification of the three
10:53:5110 hours, 53 minutes, 51 secondsdegrees of freemasonry as they answer a need. They have again prevailed although they were not existent in the Masonic
10:53:5810 hours, 53 minutes, 58 secondsform of the royal art at the beginning about two centuries ago. I say again because similar needs have already
10:54:0610 hours, 54 minutes, 6 secondsearlier produced similar forms. See Keller's writings. Whether we consider ethical education in general or the intensive introversion form of it,
10:54:1510 hours, 54 minutes, 15 secondsmysticism, we have in either case a process of development and degrees are necessary to express it symbolically.
10:54:2210 hours, 54 minutes, 22 secondsThe effort appearing from time to time to multiply the degrees has been justified. We can divide what is divided into three sections into seven also.
10:54:3210 hours, 54 minutes, 32 secondsSeven operations in alchemy, seven levels of contemplation, seven ordinations etc. although it is not
10:54:3910 hours, 54 minutes, 39 secondsreally needed. But the idea of abolishing the three degrees can only arise from a misapprehension of the value of the existing symbolism that
10:54:4810 hours, 54 minutes, 48 secondsmasonry is a union of equal rights is not affected by the presence of the degrees provided that their symbolic significance is not overstepped. The
10:54:5710 hours, 54 minutes, 57 secondsdegrees form a constituent part of the symbolic custom itself and like it are to be intangible. the symbols of all the
10:55:0410 hours, 55 minutes, 4 secondslofty spiritual religious communities for which the royal art presents itself as a paradigm or exemplar put before us
10:55:1110 hours, 55 minutes, 11 secondsas it were types of truth. Single facts which these symbols may signify or that could be read into the symbols are not
10:55:1810 hours, 55 minutes, 18 secondsthe most important but rather the totality of all these meanings. The totality which can be acquired only by a sort of integration is something
10:55:2710 hours, 55 minutes, 27 secondsinexpressable. And if it also succeeded in expressing this inexpressable, the words of the expression would be
10:55:3410 hours, 55 minutes, 34 secondsincomprehensible to any finite spirit as the individual facts are. The symbols are the unchangeable. The individual
10:55:4110 hours, 55 minutes, 41 secondsmeanings are the variegated and the changeable. As for the Masonic symbolism in particular, I am in agreement with Robert Fiser.
10:55:5010 hours, 55 minutes, 50 secondsFreemasonry rests on symbols and ceremonies. In that lies its superior title to continued existence. They are
10:55:5710 hours, 55 minutes, 57 secondscreated for eternal varities and peculiarly adapted thereto. They are fitted to every grade of culture, indeed
10:56:0510 hours, 56 minutes, 5 secondsto every time, and do not fall like other products of the time, a sacrifice to time itself. Therefore, a complete
10:56:1210 hours, 56 minutes, 12 secondsabolition of our symbols can meet with a scent as little as an infeeblement of them can be desired. Much more must we
10:56:2010 hours, 56 minutes, 20 secondsstrive in order that a clear understanding may sift out the abstract corresponding to our spiritual eye from the concrete necessary for our physical
10:56:2910 hours, 56 minutes, 29 secondseye so that the combined pictures shall be resolved in the simple fundamental truths. By this means the symbols attain
10:56:3610 hours, 56 minutes, 36 secondslife and motion and cannot be put down for things that decay with time.
10:56:4110 hours, 56 minutes, 41 secondsTherefore, the symbols should never be changed in favor of a particular meaning which becomes the fashion or be brought closer to it over and above the given
10:56:5010 hours, 56 minutes, 50 secondsrelation. What is to be maintained through variations of meaning is not the meanings but the symbols themselves.
10:56:5810 hours, 56 minutes, 58 secondsTo each person symbols represent his own truth. To everyone they speak a different language. No one exhausts
10:57:0510 hours, 57 minutes, 5 secondsthem. Everyone seeks his ideal chiefly in the unknown. It matters not so much what ideal he seeks, but only that he
10:57:1310 hours, 57 minutes, 13 secondsdoes seek one. Effort itself, not the object of effort, forms the basis of development. No seeker begins his journey with full knowledge of the goal.
10:57:2310 hours, 57 minutes, 23 secondsOnly after much circulation in the philosophic egg, and only after much passing through the prism of colors does that light dawn, which gives us the
10:57:3110 hours, 57 minutes, 31 secondsfaint intimation of the outline of the prototype of all lesser ideals. Whoever desires hope of a successful issue to
10:57:3810 hours, 57 minutes, 38 secondsthis progress must not forget a certain gentle fire that must operate from the beginning to the end, namely love. Whom
10:57:4610 hours, 57 minutes, 46 secondsthese teachings cheer not, deserves not to be a man.
